On a CREATE operation, the client\n33: \t// may omit name and rely on the server to generate the name.  If that is the case, this method will return\n34: \t// the empty string\n35: \tGetName() string\n36: \t// GetNamespace is the namespace associated with the request (if any)\n37: \tGetNamespace() string\n38: \t// GetResource is the name of the resource being requested.  This is not the kind.  For example: pods\n39: \tGetResource() schema.GroupVersionResource\n40: \t// GetSubresource is the name of the subresource being requested.  This is a different resource, scoped to the parent resource, but it may have a different kind.\n41: \t// For instance, /pods has the resource \"pods\" and the kind \"Pod\", while /pods/foo/status has the resource \"pods\", the sub resource \"status\", and the kind \"Pod\"\n42: \t// (because status operates on pods). The binding resource for a pod though may be /pods/foo/binding, which has resource \"pods\", subresource \"binding\", and kind \"Binding\".\n43: \tGetSubresource() string\n44: \t// GetOperation is the operation being performed\n45: \tGetOperation() Operation\n46: \t// GetOperationOptions is the options for the operation being performed\n47: \tGetOperationOptions() runtime.Object\n48: \t// IsDryRun indicates that modifications will definitely not be persisted for this request. This is to prevent\n49: \t// admission controllers with side effects and a method of reconciliation from being overwhelmed.\n50: \t// However, a value of false for this does not mean that the modification will be persisted, because it\n51: \t// could still be rejected by a subsequent validation step.\n52: \tIsDryRun() bool\n53: \t// GetObject is the object from the incoming request prior to default values being applied\n54: \tGetObject() runtime.Object\n55: \t// GetOldObject is the existing object. When trying to overwrite annotation with a new value, an error is returned.\n65: \t// Both ValidationInterface and MutationInterface are allowed to add Annotations.\n66: \t// By default, an annotation gets logged into audit event if the request's audit level is greater or\n67: \t// equal to Metadata.\n68: \tAddAnnotation(key, value string) error\n69: \n70: \t// AddAnnotationWithLevel sets annotation according to key-value pair with additional intended audit level.\n71: \t// An Annotation gets logged into audit event if the request's audit level is greater or equal to the\n72: \t// intended audit level.\n73: \tAddAnnotationWithLevel(key, value string, level auditinternal.Level) error\n74: \n75: \t// GetReinvocationContext tracks the admission request information relevant to the re-invocation policy.\n76: \tGetReinvocationContext() ReinvocationContext\n77: }\n78: \n79: // ObjectInterfaces is an interface used by AdmissionController to get object interfaces\n80: // such as Converter or Defaulter. \"Validate\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Pipeline\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API server admission controller system is a sophisticated pipeline that enforces policies and mutations on API requests. Here's the complete architecture:\\n\\n### Core Interface Definitions\\n\\n**File: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go**\\n\\nThis file defines the fundamental admission control interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: The base interface with a `Handles(operation Operation) bool` method that determines if a controller should process a given operation (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT).\\n- `MutationInterface`: Extends Interface and adds `Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for plugins that can mutate requests.\\n- `ValidationInterface`: Extends Interface and adds `Validate(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for plugins that only validate requests without mutations.\\n\\n### Admission Chain Execution\\n\\n**File: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go**\\n\\nThe `chainAdmissionHandler` type is a slice of Interface implementations that executes admission checks in sequence:\\n- `Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error`: Iterates through all handlers, checking if each handles the operation. For MutationInterface handlers, calls Admit and returns on first error.\\n- `Validate(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error`: Similarly iterates and calls Validate on ValidationInterface handlers.\\n- `Handles(operation Operation) bool`: Returns true if any handler handles the operation.\\n\\n### Plugin Registration and Initialization\\n\\n**File: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go**\\n\\nThe `Plugins` struct manages plugin registration and instantiation:\\n- `Register(name string, plugin Factory)`: Registers admission plugin factories with unique names.\\n- `NewFromPlugins(pluginNames []string, configProvider ConfigProvider, pluginInitializer PluginInitializer, decorator Decorator)`: Creates an admission chain from plugin names:\\n  1. Instantiates each plugin via InitPlugin\\n  2. Separates plugins into mutationPlugins and validationPlugins\\n  3. Wraps the chain with decorators (e.g., metrics)\\n  4. Returns the chain wrapped in a reinvocationHandler for webhook reinvocation support\\n\\n### Reinvocation Handler\\n\\n**File: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go**\\n\\nThe `reinvoker` wrapper handles the webhook reinvocation policy:\\n- `Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error`: Calls the wrapped admission chain's Admit method, then checks if reinvocation is needed (via `GetReinvocationContext()`) and reinvokes once if required.\\n- `Validate(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error`: Delegates directly to the wrapped chain's Validate method.\\n\\n### Configuration and Setup\\n\\n**File: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**\\n\\nThe `AdmissionOptions` struct handles admission configuration:\\n- `NewAdmissionOptions()`: Creates options with recommended plugin order: NamespaceLifecycle → MutatingAdmissionPolicy → MutatingAdmissionWebhook → ValidatingAdmissionPolicy → ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- `ApplyTo(c *server.Config, informers, kubeClient, dynamicClient, features, pluginInitializers)`: Applies admission settings to server config:\\n  1. Determines enabled plugins from flags and defaults\\n  2. Creates generic and custom plugin initializers\\n  3. Calls `NewFromPlugins` to build the complete admission chain\\n  4. Wraps the chain with metrics via `WithStepMetrics`\\n  5.
